  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:12.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">On November 15, 2021, Terns Pharmaceuticals, Inc. issued a press release announcing its financial results for the three and nine months ended September 30, 2021.   <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Terns Pharmaceuticals Reports Third Quarter 2021 Financial Results and Corporate Highlights</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">-Top-line data readout from TERN-201 (VAP-1) clinical trial in NASH expected in 1Q 2022</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">-Positive top-line data from TERN-501 (THR-&#x3b2;) demonstrated clinical proof of concept, enabling the planned initiation of NASH trial in 1H 2022</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">-Multiple abstracts detailing positive clinical data for TERN-101 and TERN-501 presented at AASLD 2021</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">-Cash and equivalents of $177 million provides runway into 2024</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">FOSTER CITY, Calif., Nov. 15, 2021 &#x2013; Terns Pharmaceuticals, Inc. (&#x201c;Terns&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Company&#x201d;) (Nasdaq: TERN), a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a portfolio of small-molecule single-agent and combination therapy candidates to address serious diseases such as non-alcoholic steatohepatitis (NASH), today reported financial results for the third quarter ended September 30, 2021 and corporate highlights.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#x201c;Recent positive clinical data for TERN-101 and TERN-501 presented at AASLD validate part one of Terns&#x2019; strategy, which is demonstrating monotherapy proof of concept. Notably, TERN-501 produced significant and dose-dependent changes in sex hormone binding globulin (SHBG), a marker of target engagement linked to NASH efficacy, suggesting that it has potential to be a best-in-class THR-&#x3b2; agonist. We look forward to the top-line data readout from the AVIATION Trial of TERN-201 in the first quarter of 2022, which could mark our third clinical candidate with promising monotherapy data,&#x201d; said Senthil Sundaram, chief executive officer at Terns. &#x201c;I am proud of the quality of execution at Terns and the momentum with which we are advancing our pipeline towards the second part of our strategy: achieving compelling and differentiated efficacy results in studies involving multiple clinically validated mechanisms of action. With this goal in mind, we are excited to move towards the planned initiation in the first half of 2022 of Terns&#x2019; first clinical trial in NASH patients including both monotherapy and combination arms of TERN-101 and TERN-501.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font>&#160;</p>

  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Top-line data from AVIATION Part 1 expected in 1Q 2022, including: </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Key efficacy readout in corrected T1 (cT1) levels, an imaging marker of liver inflammation and fibrosis linked to clinical outcomes</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Safety, tolerability and plasma VAP-1 activity </font></div></div>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:7.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">TERN-501: Thyroid hormone receptor-beta (THR-&#x3b2;) agonist</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Reported positive top-line data from Phase 1 proof of concept clinical trial in November 2021, including a presentation at AASLD 2021 demonstrating:</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Significant, dose-dependent effects on SHBG, a key pharmacodynamic marker of THR-&#x3b2; engagement linked to NASH histologic efficacy</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">TERN-501 was generally safe and well-tolerated with a predictable pharmacokinetic (PK) profile with low variability</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Significant, dose-dependent reductions in atherogenic lipids including low-density lipoprotein (LDL) cholesterol and apolipoprotein B (Apo-B) in all TERN-501 dose groups compared to placebo</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">The safety, PK and PD results support continued development of TERN-501 and indicate that it is well-suited for co-formulation with other small molecule NASH agents as an oral, once-daily fixed dose combination</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Data support plans to initiate in 1H 2022 Terns&#x2019; first NASH trial of a THR-&#x3b2; agonist (TERN-501) alone and in combination with a farnesoid X receptor (FXR) agonist (TERN-101)</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">TERN-101: Liver-distributed FXR agonist</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Presented positive data from Phase 2a LIFT clinical trial in NASH at AASLD&#x2019;s The Liver Meeting&#174; Digital Experience 2021, which demonstrated:</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">cT1 declined significantly as early as Week 6 with persistent decreases through Week 12 in all TERN-101 groups compared to placebo, with cT1 changes at Week 6 strongly correlated with changes at Week 12</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">TERN-101 treatment led to study population shifts to cT1 categories associated with lower risk of clinical events in chronic liver disease patients</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">In 10 and 15 mg groups of TERN-101, numerical reductions in alanine aminotransferase (ALT) and MRI protein density fat fraction (MRI-PDFF) were observed, with significant reductions in gamma glutamyl transferase (GGT) in all dose groups</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">TERN-101 was overall safe and well-tolerated at all doses studied with no discontinuations due to adverse events, including pruritus</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">In 5 and 10 mg groups of TERN-101, no differences from placebo in LDL cholesterol and high-density lipoprotein (HDL) cholesterol percentage change from baseline to Week 12 were observed</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">GLP1-R: Oral, small-molecule glucagon-like peptide-1 (GLP1) receptor agonist</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Driven by computational interaction mapping, chemical synthesis and </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">in vitro</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> characterization of approximately 100 GLP-1R agonist compounds; lead candidates currently undergoing higher species</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> in vivo</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> profiling</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Synthetic GLP-1 peptides have been approved for indication such as diabetes and obesity, which are conditions often accompanying NASH</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Development candidate anticipated to be designated as TERN-601 in 4Q 2021</font></div></div>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">About Terns Pharmaceuticals</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Terns Pharmaceuticals, Inc. is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a portfolio of small-molecule single-agent and combination therapy candidates to address serious diseases such as non-alcoholic steatohepatitis, or NASH. Terns&#x2019; pipeline includes three clinical stage development programs including an FXR agonist, a VAP-1 inhibitor and a THR-&#x3b2; agonist, and a preclinical small-molecule GLP-1 receptor agonist program. For more information, please visit: </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">www.ternspharma.com</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Cautionary Note Regarding Forward-Looking Statements</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">This press release contains forward-looking statements about Terns Pharmaceuticals, Inc. (the &#x201c;Company,&#x201d; &#x201c;we,&#x201d; &#x201c;us,&#x201d; or &#x201c;our&#x201d;) within the meaning of the federal securities laws, including those related to the Company&#x2019;s expectations of timing and potential results of the Company&#x2019;s clinical trials and other development activities, such as the combination trial of TERN-101 and TERN-501 and the AVIATION Trial of TERN-201 in NASH; the therapeutic potential of the Company&#x2019;s single-agent and combination therapy candidates; the potential for the mechanisms of action of the Company&#x2019;s product candidates to be therapeutic targets for NASH; the potential utility and progress of the Company&#x2019;s product candidates in NASH, including the clinical utility of the data from and the endpoints used in the Company&#x2019;s clinical trials; the Company&#x2019;s clinical development plans and activities; the Company&#x2019;s expectations regarding the profile of its product candidates, including tolerability, safety, metabolic stability and pharmacokinetic profile; the Company&#x2019;s ability to continue to execute on its clinical strategy and plans; and the Company&#x2019;s expectations with regard to its cash runway. In light of the significant uncertainties in these forward-looking statements, you should not rely upon forward-looking statements as predictions of future events. In particular, the impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on the Company&#x2019;s ability to progress with its research, development, manufacturing and regulatory efforts, including the Company&#x2019;s clinical trials for its product candidates, will depend on future developments that are highly uncertain and cannot be predicted with confidence at this time, such as the ultimate duration of the pandemic, travel restrictions, quarantines, social distancing and business closure requirements in the United States and in other countries, and the effectiveness of actions taken globally to contain and treat the disease.
